── METHODOLOGY NOTES ─────────────────────────────────────────────
  Data source       : 100% WRDS (Compustat + CRSP) — no EDGAR
  Feature source    : WRDS Compustat Q1 2025 (clean quarterly ratios)
  Delta features    : Q[t] – Q[t-1] for 10 key ratios (momentum signals)
  Label source      : yFinance adjusted closing prices Apr–Jun 2025
  Method            : VIF≤2.5 → PCA≥80% → Logistic Regression
  Winsorization     : 1st–99th percentile from training only
  Market cap ths.   : Computed from training data only
  Cluster assignment: KMeans fitted on 2010–Q3 2024, applied to Q1 2025
  Forward-looking   : Q[t] ratios → Q[t+1] outperformance (shift=-1)
  Rev/NI growth     : Q[t-1] → Q[t] change from Compustat
